Update an app configuration. This endpoint is only available to users and when using API key

  id={"request"}
  as={"h2"}

  children={"Request"}
>
</Heading>

>

  title={"Body"}
  body={{"required":true,"content":{"application/json":{"schema":{"type":"object","properties":{"appId":{"type":"number","description":"The ID of the panel application","example":1},"name":{"type":"string","description":"The name of the configuration","example":"Default View"},"level":{"description":"The level of the configuration","example":"user","allOf":[{"type":"string","enum":["user","app"],"description":"The level of the configuration","title":"AppConfigLevel"}]},"viewContent":{"type":"object","description":"The view configuration content as JSON","example":{"layout":"grid","theme":"dark"}}},"title":"UpdateAppConfigDto"}}}}}
>
  
</RequestSchema>
